[1;35r[32;1H[36m# For Unix password sync to work on a Debian GNU/Linux system, the following[39m(B[m[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;33r8[33d

[1;35r[32;1H[?25l[?12l[?25h7[2;33r8[33d
